#### Artillery Factory ####
	artillery_factory = {
		artilleryfactory0= {
			name = "artilleryfactory"
			picture = slot_artillery_factory
			
			visible = {
				check_variable = { Artillery_Buildings = 0 }
			}
			default = yes
		}
		artilleryfactory1= {
			name = "artilleryfactory"
			
			cost = @FOCUS_COST
			
			traits = { balanced_artillery_production }
			
			visible = {
				check_variable = { Artillery_Buildings = 1 }
			}
			
			equipment_bonus = {

				anti_air_equipment = {
					build_cost_ic = @LEVEL_1 instant = yes
				}
				HVanti_air_equipment = {
					build_cost_ic = @LEVEL_1 instant = yes
				}
				anti_tank_equipment = {
					build_cost_ic = @LEVEL_1 instant = yes
				}
				HVanti_tank_equipment = {
					build_cost_ic = @LEVEL_1 instant = yes
				}
				artillery_equipment = {
					build_cost_ic = @LEVEL_1 instant = yes
				}
				mountain_artillery_equipment = {
					build_cost_ic = @LEVEL_1 instant = yes
				}
				medartillery_equipment = {
					build_cost_ic = @LEVEL_1 instant = yes
				}
				Hvartillery_equipment = {
					build_cost_ic = @LEVEL_1 instant = yes

	hidden_ideas = {
	
	### AI Bonus ###
	
		training_AI = {
			allowed = {
				always = no # Triggered via event
			}

			allowed_civil_war = {
				is_ai = yes
			}
			
			modifier = {
				minimum_training_level = -0.1
				training_time_army_factor = -0.40
			}
		}
		
		AI_bonus_0 = {
			name = "AI = Basic"
			allowed = {
				always = no # Triggered via event
			}

			allowed_civil_war = {
				is_ai = yes
			}
			
			cancel = {
				OR = {
					is_ai = no 
					any_allied_country = {
						is_ai = no 
					}
				}
			}
			
			modifier = {
				line_change_production_efficiency_factor = 1
				transport_capacity = -0.5 
				political_power_gain = 0.5
				army_fuel_consumption_factor = -0.3
				air_fuel_consumption_factor = -0.3
				navy_fuel_consumption_factor = -0.5
				army_speed_factor = 0.05
				
				#ai_focus_naval_air_factor = 0
				#ai_focus_aviation_factor = 0
				#ai_focus_naval_factor = 0
				#ai_focus_peaceful_factor = 0
				#ai_focus_military_advancements_factor = 0
				#ai_focus_military_equipment_factor = 0
				#ai_focus_war_production_factor = 0
				#ai_focus_aggressive_factor = 0
				#ai_focus_defense_factor = 0
			}
		}
		
		AI_bonus_1 = {
			name = "AI = Training"
			allowed = {
				always = no # Triggered via event
			}

			allowed_civil_war = {
				is_ai = yes
			}
			
			cancel = {
				OR = {
					is_ai = no

				}
			}

				minimum_training_level = @LEVEL_5
				training_time_army_factor = -0.3
			}
		}
